                <h2 id="99999" class="accordion-title section-99999 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Disclaimer</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">NQMC Disclaimer</a></h3>
                    <p><p>The National Quality Measures Clearinghouse™ (NQMC) does not develop, produce, approve, or endorse the measures represented on this site.</p> 
<p>All measures summarized by NQMC and hosted on our site are produced under the auspices of medical specialty societies, relevant professional associations, public and private organizations, other government agencies, health care organizations or plans, individuals, and similar entities.</p> 
<p>Measures represented on the NQMC Web site are submitted by measure developers, and are screened solely to determine that they meet the <a href="/help-and-about/summaries/inclusion-criteria">NQMC Inclusion Criteria</a>.</p> 
<p>NQMC, AHRQ, and its contractor ECRI Institute make no warranties concerning the content or its reliability and/or validity of the quality measures and related materials represented on this site. Moreover, the views and opinions of developers or authors of measures represented on this site do not necessarily state or reflect those of NQMC, AHRQ, or its contractor, ECRI Institute, and inclusion or hosting of measures in NQMC may not be used for advertising or commercial endorsement purposes.</p> 
<p>Readers with questions regarding measure content are directed to contact the measure developer.</p></p>

        <div>
                <h1>End stage renal disease (ESRD): percentage of all patient-months for patients whose delivered dose of dialysis (either hemodialysis or peritoneal dialysis) met the specified threshold during the reporting period.</h1>
        </div>
    </div>

		<!-- ARTICLE -->
		<div class="article" id="article">
			




    <!-- ACCORDION -->
    <div class="accordion-container" role="tablist" multiselectable="true">
                <h2 id="563" class="accordion-title section-563 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Measure Domain</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">Primary Measure Domain</a></h3>
                    <p>Clinical Quality Measures: Outcome</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Secondary Measure Domain</a></h3>
                    <p>Does not apply to this measure</p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="566" class="accordion-title section-566 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Brief Abstract</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">Description</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>This measure is used to assess the percentage of all patient-months for patients whose delivered dose of dialysis (either hemodialysis or peritoneal dialysis) met the specified threshold during the reporting period.</p>
<p>This Kt/V dialysis adequacy comprehensive clinical measure includes the following four components:</p>
<ul style="list-style-type: disc;">
    <li>Delivered dose of hemodialysis above minimum (see the related <a href="/summaries/summary/51307" title="Measure Summary #11385" target="_blank">National Quality Measures Clearinghouse [NQMC] summary</a>) </li>
    <li>Delivered dose of peritoneal dialysis above minimum (see the related <a href="/summaries/summary/51308" title="Measure Summary #11386" target="_blank">NQMC summary</a>) </li>
    <li>Minimum single pool (sp)Kt/V for pediatric hemodialysis patients (see the related <a href="/summaries/summary/51309" title="Measure Summary #11387" target="_blank">NQMC summary</a>) </li>
    <li>Delivered dose of pediatric peritoneal dialysis above minimum (see the related <a href="/summaries/summary/51310" title="Measure Summary #11388" target="_blank">NQMC summary</a>) </li>
</ul></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Rationale</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>The primary rationale for this combined measure is to make more facilities eligible for public reporting of these metrics by meeting the greater than 11 eligible patients restriction. For public reporting on Dialysis Facility Compare (DFC) and the End Stage Renal Disease (ESRD) Quality Incentive Program (QIP), a facility has to treat at least 11 qualifying patients for each measure in order to receive a score on that measure. The 11 patient requirement is anchored in Health and Human Services (HHS) policy, related to small cell sizes to protect identification of patients and release of protected health information. An additional reason is the need for sufficient data to achieve reliability of a measure calculation for less than 11 patients. The developer recognizes there is no published evidence describing use of the combined subpopulation and modality measures. However, each component measure has strong evidence support from literature and each also reflects consensus guideline recommendations. Combining these established consensus measures to counter an unintended consequence of the application of federal protected health information regulations should not require additional scientific justification beyond what already exists.</p>
<p>In the case of dialysis adequacy, the Centers for Medicare &amp; Medicaid Services (CMS) found that a significant number of facilities that have less than 11 peritoneal dialysis (PD) patients or less than 11 pediatric patients would be included in the new combined measures but excluded from the individual measure, leading to the systematic exclusion of these facilities from assessment on these measures because of the reporting requirements.</p>
<p>To account for this, CMS proposed the three new measures that assess dialysis adequacy by modality that includes both adult and pediatric populations, and an overall measure of all adult and pediatric hemodialysis and peritoneal dialysis patients. CMS also seeks maintenance endorsement of the individual measures previously endorsed, based on the same level of evidence presented for those measures. It is CMS's intention to eventually retire the individual measures once the combined measures are endorsed and implemented.</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Evidence for Rationale</a></h3>
                    <p><table><tr><td>Centers for Medicare & Medicaid Services (CMS). CMS ESRD measures manual for the 2017 performance period: final. Version 2.5. Baltimore (MD): Centers for Medicare & Medicaid Services (CMS); 2017 Oct 11. 168 p. </td></tr></table></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Primary Health Components</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>End stage renal disease (ESRD); hemodialysis (HD); peritoneal dialysis (PD); single pool (sp)Kt/V dose; Kt/V urea dose; children; adolescents</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Denominator Description</a></h3>
                    <p><ul style="list-style-type: disc;">
    <li>All adult hemodialysis patients who received dialysis greater than two and less than four times a week (adults, greater than or equal to 18 years old), and all pediatric in-center hemodialysis patients who received dialysis greater than two and less than four times a week (pediatric, less than 18 years), and did not indicate frequent dialysis </li>
    <li>All patients (both hemodialysis and peritoneal dialysis) who are assigned to the facility for the entire month and have had end stage renal disease (ESRD) for 90 days or more </li>
</ul>
<p>See the related "Denominator Inclusions/Exclusions" field.</p></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Numerator Description</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Number of patient-months in the denominator for patients whose delivered dose of dialysis met the specified thresholds (see the related "Numerator Inclusions/Exclusions" field)</p></div></p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="573" class="accordion-title section-573 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Evidence Supporting the Measure</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">Type of Evidence Supporting the Criterion of Quality for the Measure</a></h3>
                    <p><ul><li>A clinical practice guideline or other peer-reviewed synthesis of the clinical research evidence</li><li>A systematic review of the clinical research literature (e.g., Cochrane Review)</li><li>One or more research studies published in a National Library of Medicine (NLM) indexed, peer-reviewed journal</li></ul></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Additional Information Supporting Need for the Measure</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Unspecified</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Extent of Measure Testing</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Unspecified</p></div></p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="580" class="accordion-title section-580 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">State of Use of the Measure</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">State of Use</a></h3>
                    <p>Current routine use</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Current Use</a></h3>
                    <p>External oversight/Medicare </p>
                    <p>Internal quality improvement</p>
                    <p>Pay-for-performance</p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="583" class="accordion-title section-583 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Application of the Measure in its Current Use</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">Measurement Setting</a></h3>
                    <p>Ambulatory Procedure/Imaging Center</p>
                    <p>Hospital Outpatient</p>
                    <p>Managed Care Plans</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Professionals Involved in Delivery of Health Services</a></h3>
                    <p>Physicians</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Least Aggregated Level of Services Delivery Addressed</a></h3>
                    <p>Single Health Care Delivery or Public Health Organizations</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Statement of Acceptable Minimum Sample Size</a></h3>
                    <p>Specified</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Target Population Age</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>All ages</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Target Population Gender</a></h3>
                    <p>Either male or female</p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="660" class="accordion-title section-660 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">National Strategy for Quality Improvement in Health Care</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">National Quality Strategy Aim</a></h3>
                    <p>Better Care</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">National Quality Strategy Priority</a></h3>
                    <p>Prevention and Treatment of Leading Causes of Mortality</p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="590" class="accordion-title section-590 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Institute of Medicine (IOM) National Health Care Quality Report Categories</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">IOM Care Need</a></h3>
                    <p>Living with Illness</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">IOM Domain</a></h3>
                    <p>Effectiveness</p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="593" class="accordion-title section-593 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Data Collection for the Measure</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">Case Finding Period</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>The reporting period</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Denominator Sampling Frame</a></h3>
                    <p>Patients associated with provider</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Denominator (Index) Event or Characteristic</a></h3>
                    <p>Clinical Condition</p>
                    <p>Patient/Individual (Consumer) Characteristic</p>
                    <p>Therapeutic Intervention</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Denominator Time Window</a></h3>
                    <p>Does not apply to this measure</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Denominator Inclusions/Exclusions</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p><strong>Inclusions</strong></p>
<ul style="list-style-type: disc;">
    <li>All adult hemodialysis patients who received dialysis greater than two and less than four times a week (adults, greater than or equal to 18 years old), and all pediatric in-center hemodialysis patients who received dialysis greater than two and less than four times a week (pediatric, less than 18 years), and did not indicate frequent dialysis </li>
    <li>All patients (both hemodialysis and peritoneal dialysis) who are assigned to the facility for the entire month and have had end stage renal disease (ESRD) for 90 days or more </li>
</ul>
<p class="Note"><strong>Note</strong>:</p>
<ul class="Note" style="list-style-type: disc;">
    <li>A patient may only be assigned to one dialysis facility each month. </li>
    <li>If selected Kt/V value is missing or 9.99 (i.e., when using claims), include patient-month in the denominator, but not in the numerator. </li>
    <li>If selected Kt/V value meets the Kt/V value threshold (greater than or equal to 1.2 for hemodialysis, greater than or equal to 1.7 for adult PD, or less than or equal to 1.8 for pediatric peritoneal dialysis), then include patient-month in denominator and numerator. </li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Exclusions</strong></p>
<ul style="list-style-type: disc;">
    <li>Hemodialysis patients receiving dialysis less than or equal to 2 times weekly or greater than or equal to 4 times weekly </li>
    <li>Pediatric home hemodialysis patients </li>
    <li>Patients on ESRD treatment for fewer than 90 days at the beginning of the reporting month when using CROWNWeb. If claims are used, the 90 days is determined based on the Claim-from date. </li>
    <li>Patients who changed dialysis modality during the month. Note: For adult hemodialysis patients, a change from in-center to home hemodialysis (or vice versa) is not considered a modality change. </li>
    <li>Patients who were not assigned to the facility for the entire month due to death or discharge for one of the following reasons: discontinued, involuntary discharge, transplant, or other reasons for leaving dialysis </li>
    <li>Patients who were not assigned to the facility for the entire month due to transfer to a different facility </li>
</ul></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Exclusions/Exceptions</a></h3>
                    <p>Medical factors addressed</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Numerator Inclusions/Exclusions</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p><strong>Inclusions</strong><br />
Number of patient-months in the denominator for patients whose delivered dose of dialysis met the specified thresholds. The thresholds are as follows:</p>
<ul style="list-style-type: disc;">
    <li>Hemodialysis (all ages): single pool (sp)Kt/V greater than or equal to 1.2 (calculated from the last measurement of the month using Urea Kinetic Modeling [UKM] or Daugirdas II) </li>
    <li>Peritoneal dialysis (pediatric less than 18 years old): Kt/V greater than or equal to 1.8 (dialytic + residual, measured within the past six months) </li>
    <li>Peritoneal dialysis (adult greater than or equal to 18 years old): Kt/V greater than or equal to 1.7 (dialytic + residual, measured within the past four months) </li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Exclusions</strong><br />
Unspecified</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Numerator Search Strategy</a></h3>
                    <p>Fixed time period or point in time</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Data Source</a></h3>
                    <p>Administrative clinical data</p>
                    <p>Electronic health/medical record</p>
                    <p>Registry data</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Type of Health State</a></h3>
                    <p>Physiologic Health State (Intermediate Outcome)</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Instruments Used and/or Associated with the Measure</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Kt/V Dialysis Adequacy Comprehensive Clinical Measure Rate Flowchart for ESRD QIP</p></div></p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="605" class="accordion-title section-605 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Computation of the Measure</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">Measure Specifies Disaggregation</a></h3>
                    <p>Does not apply to this measure</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Scoring</a></h3>
                    <p>Rate/Proportion</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Interpretation of Score</a></h3>
                    <p>Desired value is a higher score</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Allowance for Patient or Population Factors</a></h3>
                    <p>Does not apply to this measure</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Standard of Comparison</a></h3>
                    <p>External comparison at a point in, or interval of, time</p>
                    <p>External comparison of time trends</p>
                    <p>Internal time comparison</p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="615" class="accordion-title section-615 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Identifying Information</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">Original Title</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Kt/V dialysis adequacy comprehensive clinical measure.</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Measure Collection Name</a></h3>
                    <p>End Stage Renal Disease (ESRD) Quality Measures</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Submitter</a></h3>
                    <p>Centers for Medicare & Medicaid Services - Federal Government Agency [U.S.]</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Developer</a></h3>
                    <p>Centers for Medicare & Medicaid Services - Federal Government Agency [U.S.]</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Funding Source(s)</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Centers for Medicare &amp; Medicaid Services (CMS)</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Composition of the Group that Developed the Measure</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>The University of Michigan Kidney and Epidemiology Cost Center (UM-KECC), develops, maintains, and updates the End Stage Renal Disease (ESRD) Quality Measures for the Centers for Medicare and Medicaid Services (CMS), under the Quality Measure Development and Maintenance contract with CMS. In addition, UM-KECC works with CMS's Measures Management System (MMS) in the development, evaluation, and reporting of the current ESRD Quality Measures.</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Financial Disclosures/Other Potential Conflicts of Interest</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Unspecified</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Adaptation</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>This measure was not adapted from another source.</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Date of Most Current Version in NQMC</a></h3>
                    <p>2017 Oct</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Measure Maintenance</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Annually</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Date of Next Anticipated Revision</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Unspecified</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Measure Status</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>This is the current release of the measure.</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Source(s)</a></h3>
                    <p><table><tr><td>Centers for Medicare & Medicaid Services (CMS). CMS ESRD measures manual for the 2017 performance period: final. Version 2.5. Baltimore (MD): Centers for Medicare & Medicaid Services (CMS); 2017 Oct 11. 168 p. </td></tr></table></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Measure Availability</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Source available from the <a href="https://www.cms.gov/Medicare/Quality-Initiatives-Patient-Assessment-Instruments/ESRDQIP/Downloads/CMS-ESRD-Measures-Manual-2017.pdf"  title="Centers for Medicare &amp; Medicaid Services (CMS) Web site" target="_blank">Centers for Medicare &amp; Medicaid Services (CMS) Web site</a>&nbsp;<img alt="External Web Site Policy" src="/UI/images/icon_externallink.gif" />.</p>
<p>For more information, refer to the <a href="/Home/Disclaimer?id=51311&contentType=summary&redirect=https%3a%2f%2fdialysisdata.org%2fcontent%2fesrd-measures" title="Dialysis Data Web site">Dialysis Data Web site</a>&nbsp;<img alt="External Web Site Policy" src="/UI/images/icon_externallink.gif" /> or contact Casey Parrotte at the Kidney Epidemiology and Cost Center, The University of Michigan, 1415 Washington Heights, Suite 3645 SPHI, Ann Arbor, MI 48109-2029; Phone: 734-763-6611; Fax: 734-763-4004; Email: <a href="mailto:parrotte@med.umich.edu">parrotte@med.umich.edu</a>.</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">NQMC Status</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>This NQMC summary was completed by ECRI Institute on May 22, 2018. The information was not verified by the measure developer.</p></div></p>

		<!-- ARTICLE -->
		<div class="article" id="article">
			




    <!-- ACCORDION -->
    <div class="accordion-container" role="tablist" multiselectable="true">
                <h2 id="563" class="accordion-title section-563 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Measure Domain</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">Primary Measure Domain</a></h3>
                    <p>Related Health Care Delivery Measures: Use of Services</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Secondary Measure Domain</a></h3>
                    <p>Does not apply to this measure</p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="566" class="accordion-title section-566 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Brief Abstract</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">Description</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>This measure is used to assess the risk-adjusted standardized readmission ratio (SRR) for dialysis facility patients.</p>
<p>The SRR is defined to be the ratio of the number of Medicare-covered index discharges from acute care hospitals that resulted in an unplanned Medicare-covered readmission to an acute care hospital within 4 to 30 days of discharge for dialysis patients treated at a particular dialysis facility, to the number of readmissions that would be expected given the discharging hospitals, the characteristics of the dialysis facility's patients and the national norm for dialysis facilities.</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Rationale</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>In 2013, the Centers for Medicare and Medicaid Services (CMS) rolled out a new approach to ensuring safe and adequate health care delivery to its patients: the CMS Quality Strategy. The CMS strategy is designed to align with the six goals of the Department of Health and Human Services' (HHS) National Quality Strategy. The CMS (2013) strategy is framed in the following way: "To improve, a broad-based and seamless reform approach is necessary to address challenges in our healthcare system&mdash;escalating costs, inadequate coverage and inefficient care of variable quality." </p>
<p>Dialysis patients are a population particularly affected by such issues. Relative to the general population, they experience much higher levels of mortality (de Jager et al., 2009) and morbidity (e.g., hospital readmission; Medicare Payment Advisory Commission [MedPAC], 2007). Both hospitalization and readmission rates reflect morbidity and quality of life of dialysis patients as well as medical costs. For example, in 2011 dialysis patients were admitted to the hospital twice on average and spent an average of 12 days in the hospital, accounting for approximately 38% of Medicare expenditures for end stage renal disease (ESRD) patients (U.S. Renal Data System, 2013). Furthermore, 36% of hemodialysis patients discharged from the hospital had an unplanned readmission within 30 days (U.S. Renal Data System, 2013).</p>
<p>In the dialysis setting, care coordination strategies, including appropriate hand-off and timely pre- and post-discharge communication among care providers, have emerged as a potentially effective means to reduce unplanned readmission among the ESRD patients. A recent study in the ESRD population found that certain post-discharge assessments and changes in treatment at the dialysis facility may be associated with a reduced risk of readmission (Chan et al., 2009). A recent multi-unit qualitative study by Reilly et al. (2013) found that a lack of care coordination between in- and outpatient dialysis units post-discharge is associated with increased readmission rates. Other articles concerning the dialysis setting (Castner, 2011; Wish, 2014) discuss the importance of dialysis facility and physician communication with the discharging hospital in order to ensure appropriate coordination of care such as reconciliation of post-discharge medications and treatment orders.</p>
<p>Clinical studies in the non-ESRD populations have also demonstrated that improved care coordination and discharge planning can reduce readmission rates (Dunn et al., 1994; Bostrom et al., 1996; Dudas et al., 2001; Azevedo et al., 2002; Coleman et al., 2004; Coleman et al., 2006; Balaban et al., 2008; Braun et al., 2009) or a combination of pre- and post-discharge interventions (Naylor et al., 1994; McDonald et al., 2001; Creason, 2001; Ahmed et al., 2004; Anderson et al., 2005; Jack et al., 2009; Koehler et al., 2009; Parry et al., 2009).</p>
<p>With the U.S. healthcare system moving toward a paradigm of shared accountability across providers from different care settings, a readmission measure that is particularly applicable to ESRD patients will not only encourage improvement in transition of care across various settings, but will also serve as a strong motivation for facilities to coordinate treatment with the discharging hospital to reduce readmission rates. Such a measure should also encourage facilities to review readmission practices and identify potential problems. Moreover, measures of the frequency of unplanned readmissions are essential for controlling escalating medical costs in that they can help facilities identify problems and potentially improve care and reduce costs.</p></div></p>

                        <h3><a href="#">Primary Health Components</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>End stage renal disease (ESRD); unplanned readmission</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Denominator Description</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>The expected number of hospitalizations followed by an unplanned readmission within 4 to 30 days in each facility, which is derived from a model that accounts for patient characteristics, the dialysis facility to which the patient is discharged and the discharging hospital (see the related "Denominator Inclusions/Exclusions" field)</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Numerator Description</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Each facility's observed number of hospital discharges that are followed by an unplanned hospital readmission within 4 to 30 days of discharge (see the related "Numerator Inclusions/Exclusions" field)</p></div></p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="573" class="accordion-title section-573 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Evidence Supporting the Measure</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">Type of Evidence Supporting the Criterion of Quality for the Measure</a></h3>
                    <p><ul><li>A systematic review of the clinical research literature (e.g., Cochrane Review)</li><li>One or more research studies published in a National Library of Medicine (NLM) indexed, peer-reviewed journal</li></ul></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Additional Information Supporting Need for the Measure</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Unspecified</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Extent of Measure Testing</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Unspecified</p></div></p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="580" class="accordion-title section-580 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">State of Use of the Measure</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">State of Use</a></h3>
                    <p>Current routine use</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Current Use</a></h3>
                    <p>External oversight/Medicare </p>
                    <p>Monitoring and planning</p>
                    <p>Pay-for-performance</p>
                    <p>Public reporting</p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="583" class="accordion-title section-583 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Application of the Measure in its Current Use</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">Measurement Setting</a></h3>
                    <p>Ambulatory Procedure/Imaging Center</p>
                    <p>Hospital Inpatient</p>
                    <p>Hospital Outpatient</p>
                    <p>Managed Care Plans</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Professionals Involved in Delivery of Health Services</a></h3>
                    <p>Physicians</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Least Aggregated Level of Services Delivery Addressed</a></h3>
                    <p>Single Health Care Delivery or Public Health Organizations</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Statement of Acceptable Minimum Sample Size</a></h3>
                    <p>Does not apply to this measure</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Target Population Age</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Unspecified</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Target Population Gender</a></h3>
                    <p>Either male or female</p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="590" class="accordion-title section-590 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Institute of Medicine (IOM) National Health Care Quality Report Categories</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">IOM Care Need</a></h3>
                    <p>Not within an IOM Care Need</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">IOM Domain</a></h3>
                    <p>Not within an IOM Domain</p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="593" class="accordion-title section-593 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Data Collection for the Measure</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">Case Finding Period</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>The reporting period</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Denominator Sampling Frame</a></h3>
                    <p>Enrollees or beneficiaries</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Denominator (Index) Event or Characteristic</a></h3>
                    <p>Institutionalization</p>
                    <p>Patient/Individual (Consumer) Characteristic</p>
                    <p>Therapeutic Intervention</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Denominator Time Window</a></h3>
                    <p>Does not apply to this measure</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Denominator Inclusions/Exclusions</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p><strong>Inclusions</strong><br />
The expected number of hospitalizations followed by an unplanned readmission within 4 to 30 days in each facility, which is derived from a model that accounts for patient characteristics, the dialysis facility to which the patient is discharged and the discharging hospital.</p>
<p>The developer calculates each dialysis facility's expected number of hospitalizations followed by an unplanned readmission by fitting a model with random effects for discharging hospitals, fixed effects for facilities and regression adjustments for a set of patient-level characteristics, including measures of patient comorbidities. The developer computes the expectation for the given facility assuming readmission rates corresponding to an "average" facility with the same patient characteristics and same discharging hospitals as this facility.</p>
<p>All live discharges of dialysis patients from a Medicare-paid hospitalization in a calendar year are considered eligible for this measure.</p>
<p><strong>Exclusions</strong><br />
Hospital discharges that:</p>
<ul style="list-style-type: disc;">
    <li>Are not live discharges </li>
    <li>Result in a patient dying within 30 days with no readmission </li>
    <li>Are against medical advice </li>
    <li>Include a primary diagnosis for cancer, mental health or rehabilitation </li>
    <li>Occur after a patient's 12th admission in the calendar year </li>
    <li>Are from a Prospective Payment System (PPS)-exempt cancer hospital </li>
    <li>Result in a transfer to another hospital on the same day </li>
    <li>Result in a readmission (unplanned) within 3 days of discharge </li>
</ul></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Exclusions/Exceptions</a></h3>
                    <p>Does not apply to this measure</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Numerator Inclusions/Exclusions</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p><strong>Inclusions</strong><br />
Each facility's observed number of hospital discharges that are followed by an unplanned hospital readmission within 4 to 30 days of discharge</p>
<p class="Note"><strong>Note</strong>: Hospitalizations are counted as events in the numerator if they were followed by an unplanned readmission that (a) occurred within 4 to 30 days of a hospital discharge and (b) was not preceded by a "planned" readmission that also occurred within 4 to 30 days of discharge. In summary, a readmission is considered "planned" under two scenarios: </p>
<ol class="Note" style="list-style-type: decimal;" start="1">
    <li>The patient undergoes a procedure that is always considered planned (e.g., bone marrow transplant) or has a primary diagnosis that always indicates the hospitalization is planned (e.g., maintenance chemotherapy). </li>
    <li>The patient undergoes a procedure that MAY be considered planned if it is not accompanied by an acute diagnosis. For example, a hospitalization involving a heart valve procedure accompanied by a primary diagnosis of diabetes would be considered planned, whereas a hospitalization involving a heart valve procedure accompanied by a primary diagnosis of acute myocardial infarction (AMI) would be considered unplanned. </li>
</ol>
<p class="Note">Refer to the Planned Readmission Algorithm available from the <a href="https://www.cms.gov/Medicare/Quality-Initiatives-Patient-Assessment-Instruments/HospitalQualityInits/Measure-Methodology.html"  title="Centers for Medicare &amp; Medicaid Services Web site" target="_blank">Centers for Medicare &amp; Medicaid Services Web site</a>&nbsp;<img alt="External Web Site Policy" src="/UI/images/icon_externallink.gif" /> for additional information.</p>
<p><strong>Exclusions</strong><br />
Unspecified</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Numerator Search Strategy</a></h3>
                    <p>Institutionalization</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Data Source</a></h3>
                    <p>Administrative clinical data</p>
                    <p>Registry data</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Type of Health State</a></h3>
                    <p>Proxy for Outcome</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Instruments Used and/or Associated with the Measure</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Unspecified</p></div></p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="605" class="accordion-title section-605 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Computation of the Measure</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">Measure Specifies Disaggregation</a></h3>
                    <p>Does not apply to this measure</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Scoring</a></h3>
                    <p>Ratio</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Interpretation of Score</a></h3>
                    <p>Desired value is a lower score</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Allowance for Patient or Population Factors</a></h3>
                    <p>Risk adjustment devised specifically for this measure/condition</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Description of Allowance for Patient or Population Factors</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>The risk adjustment approach used in the model for this measure was adapted from Center for Medicare &amp; Medicaid Services' (CMS's) standardized hospitalization ratio (SHR) and CMS's Hospital-Wide Readmission (HWR) measure. The regression model used to compute a facility's "expected" number of readmissions for this measure contains many factors thought to be associated with readmission event rates. Specifically, the model adjusts for age, sex, diabetes, duration of end stage renal disease (ESRD), body mass index (BMI) at start of dialysis, past-year comorbidities, length of the index hospital stay, and the presence of a high-risk diagnosis at index discharge. In addition, the model adjusts for the effect of the discharging hospital (via random effects). Refer to the original measure documentation for additional details.</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Standard of Comparison</a></h3>
                    <p>External comparison at a point in, or interval of, time</p>
                    <p>External comparison of time trends</p>
                    <p>Internal time comparison</p>

            </div>
                <h2 id="615" class="accordion-title section-615 is-active" role="tab" aria-expanded="true"><a href="#">Identifying Information</a></h2>
            <div class="accordion-panel is-active" role="tabpanel">
                        <h3><a href="#">Original Title</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Standardized readmissions ratio (SRR) clinical measure.</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Measure Collection Name</a></h3>
                    <p>End Stage Renal Disease (ESRD) Quality Measures</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Submitter</a></h3>
                    <p>Centers for Medicare & Medicaid Services - Federal Government Agency [U.S.]</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Developer</a></h3>
                    <p>Centers for Medicare & Medicaid Services - Federal Government Agency [U.S.]</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Funding Source(s)</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Center for Medicare &amp; Medicaid Services (CMS)</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Composition of the Group that Developed the Measure</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Unspecified</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Financial Disclosures/Other Potential Conflicts of Interest</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Unspecified</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Endorser</a></h3>
                    <p>National Quality Forum</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">NQF Number</a></h3>
                    <p>2496</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Date of Endorsement</a></h3>

                        <h3><a href="#">Measure Initiative(s)</a></h3>
                    <p>Dialysis Facility Compare (DFC)</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Adaptation</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>This measure was not adapted from another source.</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Date of Most Current Version in NQMC</a></h3>
                    <p>2017 Oct</p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Measure Maintenance</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Annually</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Date of Next Anticipated Revision</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Unspecified</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Measure Status</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>This is the current release of the measure.</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Source(s)</a></h3>
                    <p><table><tr><td>Centers for Medicare & Medicaid Services (CMS). CMS ESRD measures manual for the 2017 performance period: final. Version 2.5. Baltimore (MD): Centers for Medicare & Medicaid Services (CMS); 2017 Oct 11. 168 p. </td></tr></table></p>
                    <p><table><tr><td>Centers for Medicare & Medicaid Services (CMS). Measure information form: dialysis facility compare -- standardized readmission ratio. Baltimore (MD): Centers for Medicare & Medicaid Services (CMS); 2016 Oct. 11 p. </td></tr></table></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">Measure Availability</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>Source available from the <a href="https://www.cms.gov/Medicare/Quality-Initiatives-Patient-Assessment-Instruments/ESRDQIP/Downloads/CMS-ESRD-Measures-Manual-2017.pdf"  title="Centers for Medicare &amp; Medicaid Services (CMS) Web site" target="_blank">Centers for Medicare &amp; Medicaid Services (CMS) Web site</a>&nbsp;<img alt="External Web Site Policy" src="/UI/images/icon_externallink.gif" />.</p>
<p>For more information, refer to the <a href="/Home/Disclaimer?id=51313&contentType=summary&redirect=https%3a%2f%2fdialysisdata.org%2fcontent%2fesrd-measures" title="Dialysis Data Web site">Dialysis Data Web site</a>&nbsp;<img alt="External Web Site Policy" src="/UI/images/icon_externallink.gif" /> or contact Casey Parrotte at the Kidney Epidemiology and Cost Center, The University of Michigan, 1415 Washington Heights, Suite 3645 SPHI, Ann Arbor, MI 48109-2029; Phone: 734-763-6611; Fax: 734-763-4004; Email: <a href="mailto:parrotte@med.umich.edu">parrotte@med.umich.edu</a>.</p></div></p>
                        <h3><a href="#">NQMC Status</a></h3>
                    <p><div class="content_para"><p>This NQMC summary was completed by ECRI Institute on May 22, 2018. The information was not verified by the measure developer.</p></div></p>
